<p>Welcome to MailaAI. These Terms of Service ("Terms") govern your access to and use of the websites, products, APIs, software, tools, and other services (collectively, the "Services") provided by MailaAI ("MailaAI", "we", "us", or "our"). <p>MailaAI collaborates with various third-party service providers to ensure the efficient and secure delivery of our Services to you. These providers are carefully chosen for their expertise and capabilities in supporting the functionalities and features that MailaAI offers. It's important to note that in the process of delivering these services, your data may be processed or pass through the systems of these service providers. Below is a list of our key service providers:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>OpenAI</strong>: Specializes in advanced AI technologies and models. <a href="https://openai.com/privacy/">Privacy Policy</a>
<ul>
<li><strong>Microsoft</strong>: Offers cloud computing services, including Azure, and various other technology solutions. <a href="https://privacy.microsoft.com/en-us/privacystatement">Privacy Policy</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Amazon Web Services (AWS)</strong>: Provides a broad set of global cloud-based products. <a href="https://aws.amazon.com/privacy/">Privacy Policy</a></li>
<li><strong>Google Cloud Platform (GCP)</strong>: Offers a suite of cloud computing services. <a href="https://cloud.google.com/terms/cloud-privacy-notice">Privacy Policy</a></li>
<li><strong>Anthropic</strong>: Focuses on AI safety and research. <a href="https://www.anthropic.com/privacy-policy">Privacy Policy</a></li>
<li><strong>Vercel</strong>: A cloud platform for static sites and Serverless Functions. <a href="https://vercel.com/legal/privacy-policy">Privacy Policy</a></li>
</ul>
<p>By using MailaAI's Services, you acknowledge and agree that your data may be processed by these service providers as part of the service delivery. MailaAI ensures that all service providers are compliant with our data protection standards and policies to safeguard your data's privacy and security.</p>

<h3 id="professional-review" style="position:relative;"><a href="#professional-review" aria-label="professional review permalink" class="anchor before"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Professional Review</h3>
<p>If you are a business using the Services to generate content related to legal, medical, financial, or other professional advice, you must ensure that:</p>
<ul>

<li>The content complies with all applicable laws, regulations, and professional standards in your jurisdiction</li>

<h3 id="human-in-the-loop" style="position:relative;"><a href="#human-in-the-loop" aria-label="human in the loop permalink" class="anchor before"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Human-in-the-Loop</h3>
<p>Businesses using the Services for customer interactions or decision-making processes must ensure that there is meaningful human involvement and oversight in the loop. This includes:</p>
<ul>
<li>Regularly reviewing and auditing the outputs generated by the Services</li>
<li>Providing clear escalation paths for users to request human review or appeal automated decisions</li>
<li>Ensuring that humans retain ultimate control and accountability for significant decisions</li>
</ul>

<ul>

<li>Identification of the allegedly infringing material and its location on the Services</li>

</ul>
<h3 id="counter-notification-procedures" style="position:relative;"><a href="#counter-notification-procedures" aria-label="counter notification procedures permalink" class="anchor before"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Counter-Notification Procedures</h3>
<p>If you believe that your content was removed from the Services due to a mistake or misidentification, you may submit a counter-notification to MailaAI's designated agent. The counter-notification must include:</p>
<ul>
<li>Identification of the material that has been removed and its former location on the Services</li>
<li>Your contact information, including name, address, telephone number, and email address</li>
<li>A statement under penalty of perjury that you have a good faith belief that the material was removed by mistake or misidentification</li>
<li>A statement that you consent to the jurisdiction of the court in which your address is located</li>
<li>Your physical or electronic signature</li>
</ul>
<p>Upon receiving a valid counter-notification, MailaAI will promptly forward it to the party who submitted the original takedown notice. If MailaAI does not receive notice within 10 business days that the original complainant is seeking a court order to prevent further infringement, MailaAI may restore the removed material to the Services.</p>

<h3 id="data-storage-location" style="position:relative;"><a href="#data-storage-location" aria-label="data storage location permalink" class="anchor before"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Data Storage Location</h3>
<p>MailaAI stores and processes your data in data centers located in Sweden and other countries where MailaAI or its service providers maintain facilities. By using the Services, you consent to the transfer of your data to countries outside of your country of residence, which may have different data protection laws.</p>
<h3 id="discord-data" style="position:relative;"><a href="#discord-data" aria-label="discord data permalink" class="anchor before"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Discord Data</h3>
<p>If you interact with MailaAI through Discord, any data you provide through direct messages or other interactions with the MailaAI Discord bot is stored on Discord's servers and subject to Discord's privacy practices. MailaAI has limited ability to access or delete data stored by Discord.</p>
<h3 id="sale-of-personal-data" style="position:relative;"><a href="#sale-of-personal-data" aria-label="sale of personal data permalink" class="anchor before"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Sale of Personal Data</h3>
<p>MailaAI does not sell your personal data to third parties. More information about MailaAI's data handling practices is available in our Privacy Policy.</p>
<h3 id="data-deletion-requests" style="position:relative;"><a href="#data-deletion-requests" aria-label="data deletion requests permalink" class="anchor before"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Data Deletion Requests</h3>
<p>You have the right to request the deletion of your personal data from MailaAI's systems, subject to certain exceptions permitted by law. Upon receiving a verifiable deletion request, MailaAI will delete your personal data from our records and direct our service providers to do the same, unless an exception applies. Exceptions may include cases where the data is necessary to comply with legal obligations.</p>
<hr>
<h2 id="38-data-deletion-process" style="position:relative;"><a href="#38-data-deletion-process" aria-label="38 data deletion process permalink" class="anchor before"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>38. Data Deletion Process</h2>
<h3 id="eligibility-for-data-deletion" style="position:relative;"><a href="#eligibility-for-data-deletion" aria-label="eligibility for data deletion permalink" class="anchor before"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Eligibility for Data Deletion</h3>
<p>MailaAI will honor data deletion requests for personal data that is no longer necessary for the purposes for which it was collected, or where the processing is based on consent and you have withdrawn your consent. However, MailaAI may retain certain data as necessary for legitimate business purposes or to comply with legal obligations.</p>
<h3 id="required-information" style="position:relative;"><a href="#required-information" aria-label="required information permalink" class="anchor before"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Required Information</h3>
<p>To submit a data deletion request, please provide the following information:</p>
<ul>
<li>Your full name and email address associated with your MailaAI account</li>
<li>A clear and specific description of the personal data you want deleted</li>
<li>Any additional information that may be necessary to verify your identity and locate your data</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="response-timeframe" style="position:relative;"><a href="#response-timeframe" aria-label="response timeframe permalink" class="anchor before"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Response Timeframe</h3>
<p>MailaAI will acknowledge receipt of your data deletion request within 30 business days and provide an estimated timeframe for processing the request. In most cases, MailaAI will complete the deletion within 60 days of receiving a verifiable request. If MailaAI requires more time, you will be notified of the reason and extension period.</p>
<p>MailaAI may request additional information from you to verify your identity and ensure that you are authorized to make the deletion request. MailaAI will notify you once the deletion process is complete.</p>

<h2 id="39-definitions" style="position:relative;"><a href="#39-definitions" aria-label="39 definitions permalink" class="anchor before"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" height="16" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>39. Definitions</h2>
